# Text Elements
It means that the rate of forwards reaction
is equal to the rate of backward reaction - 1
The concentration on both side, stays 
constant - 1 ^m5fgEXVK

The increase in temperature prefers the 
endothermic side, hence the reverse reaction
must be endothermic ^aeLVozE7

Decrease in pressure would influence the
position to go on the more moles side ^pHh6Z5QJ

The reaction becomes more dark brown. ^q5MmQTl2

Energy Change = -23kj/mol ^bGNogDt1

The rate of forward reaction is equal to the rate of backward reaction
the concentration on both side stays constant ^qpdTJKmx

Increase ^ZT0gyK13

An increase in pressure prefers the side with the least moles
and as Reaction 2's products had less moles. That is the answer ^ZdevVsgm

Constant ^BsjL2p2N

Reaction 1 ^B8mVzvXw

The amount of moles on both side is same, Hence pressure has no affect ^bpSUvutL

Decreases ^ohkpvf0T

Reaction 3 ^1IaCR9MU

As the reactant side has less moles, It is preferred
and the product side has less % formed  ^3wUkpdcf
